+    for macro in options.rpmmacros:
+        try:
+            k, v = macro.split(" ", 1)
+            if not k.startswith('%'):
+                k = '%%%s' % k
+            config_opts['macros'].update({k: v})
+        except:
+            raise mock.exception.BadCmdline(
+                "Bad option for '--define' (%s).  Use --define 'name value'"
+                % macro)
